<p><a href="/wiki/MediaWiki:Gadgets-definition" title="MediaWiki:Gadgets-definition">Definitions</a> · <a href="/wiki/Special:Gadgets" title="Special:Gadgets">Descriptions</a>
</p>
</div>
<p>Below is a list of custom features ("<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Gadget" title="Wikipedia:Gadget">gadgets</a>") you may enable for your account.  Most of them require JavaScript to be enabled in your browser. Please note that these tools are not part of the MediaWiki software, and are usually developed and maintained by users on Wikipedia. Some options are only available for certain <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Skin" title="Wikipedia:Skin">skins</a>. The numbers of users for each gadget on this wiki are listed at <a href="/wiki/Special:GadgetUsage" title="Special:GadgetUsage">Gadget usage statistics</a>.
</p><p>Gadget legend:
</p>
<ul><li><sup><abbr title="Enabled for everyone by default.">(D)</abbr></sup>: These gadgets are enabled by <u>d</u>efault</li>
<li><sup><abbr title="Loads code from an external project not governed by the WMF Privacy Policy">(E)</abbr></sup>: These gadgets use code from <u>e</u>xternal (third party) systems not subject to the WMF Privacy Policy</li>
<li><sup><abbr title="Loads code managed on another WMF project">(S)</abbr></sup>: These gadgets use code from WMF <u>s</u>ister projects, managed by that project's administrators</li>
<li><sup><abbr title="Loads code subject to change by a single user">(U)</abbr></sup>: These gadgets use code maintained by a single <u>u</u>ser</li></ul>

For more information see our <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Policies_and_guidelines" title="Wikipedia:Policies and guidelines">policies and guidelines</a></b>.</td></tr></tbody></table></label></div></div></div><div class='mw-htmlform-field-HTMLMultiSelectField  oo-ui-layout oo-ui-fieldLayout oo-ui-fieldLayout-align-top'><div </p><p>The <a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Extension:CirrusSearch/CompletionSuggester">completion suggester</a> is an algorithm for search suggestions with better typo correction and search relevance. Certain platform notices, such as those relating to site maintenance and special notices considered necessary to all users, will always be displayed. For further information, please read the &lt;a href=\"https:\/\/meta.wikimedia.org\/wiki\/Special:MyLanguage\/CentralNotice\" class=\"extiw\" title=\"metawikimedia:Special:MyLanguage\/CentralNotice\"&gt;documentation on Meta-Wiki&lt;\/a&gt;.\n&lt;\/p&gt;"}}'><p>Banners display announcements of interest to Wikimedia communities and users.
</p><p>Below are options that allow you to manage which types of announcements you see. Certain platform notices, such as those relating to site maintenance and special notices considered necessary to all users, will always be displayed. For further information, please read the <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/CentralNotice" class="extiw" title="metawikimedia:Special:MyLanguage/CentralNotice">documentation on Meta-Wiki</a>.
</p></label></div></div></div>

class="mw-ui-feature-user-count">24,408 users are trying this feature.</p><p class="mw-ui-feature-description"><p>Enables experimental talk page features:
</p>
<ul><li><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Talk_pages_project/Replying">Reply</a> to talk page comments with one click.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Talk_pages_project/New_discussion">Add new topics</a> using an inline form.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Talk_pages_project/Notifications">Receive notifications</a> when new comments are added in sections you have subscribed to.</li></ul>
<p>You can customize these features in your <a href="/wiki/Special:Preferences#mw-prefsection-editing-discussion" title="Special:Preferences">preferences</a>.
</p><p>Updates will be posted on the <a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Talk_pages_project/Updates">talk pages project's updates page</a>.
</p><p>Please note:
</p>
<ul><li>Over time, new experimental features will be added.</li>
<li>Some of the features above may not be available at your wiki yet.</li></ul></p><ul class="mw-ui-feature-requirements-list"><li class="mw-ui-feature-requirements-javascript">This feature requires class="mw-ui-feature-main"><div class="mw-ui-feature-meta"><p class="mw-ui-feature-user-count">167,137 users are trying this feature.</p><p class="mw-ui-feature-description">A <a
